<p><b>аф<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ри<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:кан.html>ка́н</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ский</b>

</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-африк-</b>; интерфикс: <b>-ан-</b>; суффикс: <b>-ск</b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ий</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.

***аффект.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:аффект.html>аффе́кт</a> (28410)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:аффект.html>аффе́кт</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">affékt</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:аффект.html>аффе́кта</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:аффект.html>аффе́кты</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:аффект.html>аффе́ктов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">law</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> temporary insanity, irresistible impulse</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">psychology</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> affect <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">feeling in response to a stimulus</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>

<p><b>аф<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>фе́кт</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:существительное.html>Существи́тельное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:неодушевленный.html>неодушевлённое</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:мужской.html>мужско́й</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:род.html>род</a>, 2-е <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ние</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> 1a  <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка).

***ахнуть.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ахнуть.html>а́хнуть</a> (4890)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Perhaps from <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ахать.html>а́хать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">áxatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-нуть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nutʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> or <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ах.html>ах́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ax</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-нуть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nutʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>; since the 18th century.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ахнуть.html>а́хнуть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">áxnutʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ахать.html>а́хать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to exclaim, to gasp, to sigh
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>он</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:так.html>так</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:ахнуть.html>а́хнул</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">on tak i <b>áxnul</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">he simply opened his mouth</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:ахнуть.html>а́хнуть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:от.html>от́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:удивление.html>удивле́ния</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>áxnutʹ</b> ot udivlénija</i> ― <span class="e-translation">gasp with surprise</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>он</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:ахнуть.html>а́хнуть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:успеть.html>успе́л</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">on i <b>áxnutʹ</b> ne uspél</i> ― <span class="e-translation"> before he knew where he was; before he could say knife</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:баба.html>ба́ба</a> (837)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_7">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*baba</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_8">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:баба.html>ба́ба</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">bába</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr> or <abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:баба.html>ба́бы</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:баба.html>ба́бы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:баба.html>баб</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">childish</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> grandma, granny <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">short for <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бабушка.html>ба́бушка</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">bábuška</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мама.html>ма́ма</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>а</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:где.html>где</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:баба.html>ба́ба</a></b>?</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Máma, a gde <b>bába</b>?</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Mom, where’s grandma?</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">informal or archaic</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> old woman <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">short for <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бабушка.html>ба́бушка</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">bábuška</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru">жи́ли-бы́ли <a href = vnd.unilang:дед.html>дед</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:да.html>да</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:баба.html>ба́ба</a></b>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Žíli-býli ded da <b>bába</b>.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">There once lived an old man and his old woman.</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">historical</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> (any) woman; countrywoman</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial<span class="ib-comma">,</span> slang<span class="ib-comma">,</span> derogatory</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> woman, female, broad; countrywoman
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кто.html>Кто</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:этот.html>э́та</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:баба.html>ба́ба</a></b>?</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Kto éta <b>bába</b>?</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Who's that broad?</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:весь.html>Все</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:баба.html>ба́бы</a></b> — <a href = vnd.unilang:дура.html>ду́ры</a>; <a href = vnd.unilang:весь.html>все</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:мужик.html>мужики́</a> — <a href = vnd.unilang:сволочь.html>сво́лочи</a></i> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">contemporary Russian saying</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Vse <b>báby</b> — dúry; vse mužikí — svóloči</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">"Every woman is stupid, every man is a bastard"</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> peasant’s wife, peasant woman</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">derogatory</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> milksop, old woman <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">weak man</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">technical</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> ram <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of a pile driver</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">technical</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> drop weight</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">cooking</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> baba <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">tall, cylindrical cake</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>, bundt cake, Gugelhupf
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru">ро́мовая <b><a href = vnd.unilang:баба.html>ба́ба</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">rómovaja <b>bába</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">rum baba, rum cake</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="use-with-mention">in expressions</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:снежный.html>сне́жная</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:баба.html>ба́ба</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">snéžnaja <b>bába</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">snowman</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:каменный.html>ка́менная</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:баба.html>ба́ба</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">kámennaja <b>bába</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">primitive stone statue</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:ба.html>ба́</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:ба.html>ба</a></b>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:бабахнуть.html>баба́хнувший</a> (30922)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*babъka</i>.

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бабка.html>ба́бка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">bábka</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бабка.html>ба́бки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бабка.html>ба́бки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бабка.html>ба́бок</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>old woman, crone</li>

***бабочка.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:бабочка.html>ба́бочка</a> (4830)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бабка.html>ба́бка</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">bábka</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">old woman, grandmother</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ка</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, originally a diminutive; from the folk belief that spirits of the dead live on as butterflies.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бабочка.html>ба́бочка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">bábočka</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr> or <abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бабочка.html>ба́бочки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бабочка.html>ба́бочки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бабочка.html>ба́бочек</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>butterfly
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ночной.html>ночна́я</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:бабочка.html>ба́бочка</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">nočnája <b>bábočka</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">moth</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>bowtie</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> feisty, spirited woman</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> prostitute, hooker</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p>Russian does not divide butterflies and moths the same way English does. Russian has <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мотылек.html>мотылёк</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">motyljók</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> for a kind of small moth that swarms at night, and <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:моль.html>моль</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">molʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> for the moth that eats clothes, but the other moths are all <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бабочка.html>ба́бочки</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">bábočki</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:ба.html>ба́</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>боч<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ка</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:существительное.html>Существи́тельное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:одушевленный.html>одушевлённое</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:женский.html>же́нский</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:род.html>род</a>, 1-е <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ние</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> 3*a  <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка).
<a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>В</a> знач. <i><a href = vnd.unilang:галстук.html>галстук</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:слово.html>сло́во</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склоняться.html>склоня́ется</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:образец.html>образцу́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:для.html>для</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:неодушевленный.html>неодушевлённых</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:существительное.html>существи́тельных</a> (<span title="в винительном падеже"><a href = vnd.unilang:кто.html>кого́</a>/<a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>что</a>?</span> — <i><a href = vnd.unilang:бабочка.html>ба́бочку</a></i>, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:бабочка.html>бабочки</a></i>).
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-бабочк-</b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b><a href = vnd.unilang:понимать.html>-а</a></b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*babušьka</i>. Synchronically analyzable as <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:баба.html>ба́ба</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">bába</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ушка</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-uška</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бабушка.html>ба́бушка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">bábuška</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бабушка.html>ба́бушки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бабушка.html>ба́бушки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бабушка.html>ба́бушек</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>grandmother, grandma, granny
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рассказать.html>расскажи́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́то</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:свое.html>свое́й</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:бабушка.html>ба́бушке</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">rasskaží éto svojéj bábuške</i> ― <span class="e-translation">tell it to Sweeney, tell it to the marines</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>old lady</li></ol>
